He emerged victorious in the competition by answering “Finnmark” to the question, “One-third of Norway’s northernmost country is in what plateau?” However, winning this game was far from easy. Janga fought tooth and nail with Mallanna, a sixth-grader at William Diamond Middle School in Lexington, Massachusetts, to claim the title. Even last year, three Indian American students scooped the top three positions in the National Geographic GeoBee competition.
